Notice	
	
..	
434
Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

public Notices
	
M. Saravanabava, a male child son of Thiru R. Mohan, born on 2nd February 1996, residing at No. 2/131, South 
Street, Umbalappadi, Papanasam Taluk, Thanjavur-614 203.  Has been living as female. I have been granted Identity Card 
No. KPM/073/2019 issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. 
By this I, may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as M. YAZHINI
Thanjavur,	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
M. SARAVANABAVA
24th February 2020.
